Abstract: This paper considers constrained stochastic nonsmooth minimax optimization problem of the form $\min_{\mathbf{x}\in\mathcal{X}}\max_{\mathbf{y}\in\mathcal{Y}}f\left(\mathbf{x},\mathbf{y}\right)=\mathbb{E}[F(\mathbf{x},\mathbf{y};\mathbfξ)]$, where the objective $f(\mathbf{x},\mathbf{y})$ is concave in $\mathbf{y}$ but possibly nonconvex in $\mathbf{x}$, the stochastic component $F(\mathbf{x},\mathbf{y};\mathbfξ)$ indexed by random variable $\mathbfξ$ is mean-squared Lipschitz continuous, and the feasible sets $\mathcal X$ and $\mathcal Y$ are convex and compact. We introduce the notion of $(η_x,η_y,δ,ε)$-Goldstein saddle stationary point (GSSP) to characterize the convergence for solving constrained nonsmooth minimax problems. We then develop projected gradient-free descent ascent methods for finding $(η_x,η_y,δ,ε)$-GSSPs of the objective function $f(\mathbf{x},\mathbf{y})$ with non-asymptotic convergence rates. We further propose nested-loop projected gradient-free descent ascent methods to establish the non-asymptotic convergence for finding $(η,δ,ε)$-generalized Goldstein stationary points (GGSP) [Liu et al., 2024] of the primal function $Φ(\mathbf{x})\triangleq\max_{\mathbf{y}\in\mathcal{Y}}{f}\left(\mathbf{x},\mathbf{y}\right)$. It is worth noting that our algorithm designs and theoretical analyses do not require additional assumptions such as the weak convexity used in prior works on nonsmooth minimax optimization [Lin et al., 2025, Boţ and Böhm, 2023].

Result: 首次建立了SOAP优化器的收敛速率，并将其收敛性结果推广到了更一般的变体上。

Conclusion: 本文为SOAP及其变体提供了理论收敛保证，为这类基于矩阵的优化器的应用提供了理论基础。

Abstract: In this short note, we establish, for the first time, the convergence rate of SOAP, an efficient and popular matrix-based optimizer for training deep neural networks. Our analysis extends to a more general variant of SOAP that admits arbitrary orthogonal projection matrices and requires only that these matrices be conditionally independent of the current stochastic gradient at each iteration. For example, they may be constructed from information available up to the preceding step.

</details>


### [167] [Robust mean field control: stochastic maximum principle and variational mean field games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21641)
*François Delarue,Pierre Lavigne*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一类最小-最大形式的鲁棒控制问题，其中主智能体被视为面临自然的中央规划者。智能体的成本是其所有可能实现的非线性函数，特别包括平均场情形。自然以熵成本支持对智能体最不利的结果。在适当的凸性-凹性条件下，建立了解的存在唯一性，并推导了相关的随机最大值原理。进一步研究了交互项存在模糊性的鲁棒变分平均场博弈，证明了其解的存在唯一性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将鲁棒控制问题形式化为最小-最大框架，使主智能体与自然形成对抗关系，同时处理成本函数的非线性依赖性（包括平均场情形），并考虑自然以熵成本选择最不利结果的机制。

Method: 采用最小-最大鲁棒控制框架，建立凸性-凹性条件确保解的存在唯一性，推导随机最大值原理；将方法拓展至鲁棒变分平均场博弈，处理交互项的模糊性。

Result: 在适当的凸性-凹性假设下，证明了鲁棒控制问题解的存在唯一性；得到了相关的随机最大值原理；证明了鲁棒变分平均场博弈解的存在唯一性。

Conclusion: 所提出的最小-最大鲁棒控制框架能有效处理智能体成本对状态分布的非线性依赖，以及自然对抗性选择带来的模糊性，且该框架可成功拓展至平均场博弈中的交互项模糊性问题。

Abstract: We introduce a class of robust control problems formulated in min-max form, in which the principal agent is viewed as a central planner facing Nature. The agent's cost is a nonlinear function of all its possible realizations, encompassing in particular the mean field regime where the cost depends on the distribution of the states. In parallel, Nature favors the occurrence of outcomes that are least favorable to the agent, at an entropic cost. We establish existence and uniqueness of solutions under appropriate assumptions, including suitable convexity-concavity conditions, and derive a related stochastic maximum principle. We further address a corresponding class of robust variational mean field games in which the interaction term is subject to ambiguity, and prove existence and uniqueness of solutions.

</details>


### [168] [Optimal control of therapies related to an oxytaxis glioblastoma model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21674)
*Juan J. Forero-Hernańdez,Francisco Guillén-González,Élder J. Villamizar-Roa*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出并分析了一个与Keller-Segel型抛物系统相关的最优控制问题，该问题模拟了二维有界域中受氧浓度影响的胶质母细胞瘤生长，其中控制变量为化疗和抗血管生成两种疗法。研究建立了弱-强解的存在唯一性理论框架，证明了全局最优解的存在性并推导了一阶最优性必要条件，最后通过伴随方法和Adam梯度优化方法实现了数值近似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立胶质母细胞瘤生长的数学模型，并优化化疗与抗血管生成疗法的联合治疗方案，以最小化肿瘤生长和氧浓度。

Method: 采用Keller-Segel型抛物系统建模肿瘤细胞趋氧运动，建立弱-强解存在唯一性理论框架；通过伴随方法推导最优控制的一阶必要条件，并利用Adam梯度优化算法对缩减成本泛函进行数值最小化。

Result: 证明了全局最优解的存在性，推导了最优性条件，并通过数值实验验证了所提方案的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文为胶质母细胞瘤的联合治疗优化提供了严格的理论基础与可行的数值求解方法。

Abstract: We propose and analyze an optimal control problem associated with a Keller-Segel type parabolic system with chemoattraction, modeling the glioblastoma growth in a bi-dimensional bounded domain, influenced by the presence of oxygen where the controls are two different (chemotherapy and antiangiogenic) therapies. The model considers the random diffusion of tumor cells and oxygen, the movement of cells towards the oxygen gradient (oxytaxis), and reaction terms describing the interaction between cells and oxygen. We establish a mathematical framework to analyze the existence and uniqueness of weak-strong solution of the model and subsequently we analyze an optimal control problem considering a cost functional that minimizes both the tumor growth and the oxygen concentration. We prove the existence of a global optimal solution and derive necessary first-order optimality conditions. Finally, we propose a methodology for approximating the optimal therapies. We use the gradient of the reduced cost functional through the adjoint scheme, and minimize the cost functional implementing the Adam gradient optimization method. Some numerical experiments are provided to demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed scheme.

</details>


### [169] [$H_2/H_{\infty}$ Control for Stochastic Differential Systems with Partial Observation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21799)
*Changwang Xiao,Nan Yang,Qingxin Meng*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文研究了部分观测下线性随机微分系统的H₂/H∞控制问题，通过卡尔曼滤波和交叉耦合Riccati方程，建立了部分观测框架下的随机有界实引理，并证明了纳什均衡存在性与方程可解性之间的关联，通过无人机仿真验证了方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究假设控制器可获取完整状态信息，而实际系统中控制器通常只能通过观测过程获取部分信息。本文旨在解决部分观测条件下线性随机微分系统的H₂/H∞控制问题，填补该领域的理论空白。

Method: 将H₂/H∞控制问题建模为非零和微分博弈；利用卡尔曼滤波方法推导最优滤波方程；建立部分观测框架下的随机有界实引理；通过交叉耦合Riccati方程刻画纳什均衡存在的充要条件。

Result: 得到了部分观测下H∞鲁棒约束的充要条件（随机有界实引理）；揭示了纳什均衡存在性与交叉耦合Riccati方程可解性之间的联系；无人机数值算例验证了方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文为部分观测下线性随机系统的H₂/H∞控制提供了完整的理论框架，所提方法能够有效平衡H₂性能与H∞鲁棒性要求，且适用于实际工程系统（如无人机）。

Abstract: This paper investigates the $H_{2}/H_{\infty}$ control problem for linear stochastic differential systems under partial observation. Unlike existing studies that assume full state accessibility, we consider the scenario where the controller has access only to an observation process. The objective is to design a controller that balances the $H_2$ performance criterion with the $H_\infty$ robustness requirement under worst-case disturbances, formulated as a nonzero-sum differential game. Using the Kalman filtering method, we derive the corresponding optimal filtering equation. Furthermore, a Stochastic Bounded Real Lemma under the partial observation framework is established, providing necessary and sufficient conditions for the $H_\infty$ robustness constraint. We also show the connection between the existence of a Nash equilibrium and the solvability of the cross-coupled Riccati equations, and illustrate the effectiveness of the proposed approach through a numerical example involving an unmanned aerial vehicle (UAV).

</details>
